src/cli/main.py:261:def pipeline(ctx, keywords, template, var, company, location, max_pages, mode, dry_run, skip_messaged, batch_pages, interactive, resume):
src/cli/main.py:262:    """
src/cli/main.py:263:    Search candidates and batch send messages in one command.
src/cli/main.py:264:
src/cli/main.py:265:    Combines multi-keyword search with batch messaging:
src/cli/main.py:266:    search → preview → confirm → send.
src/cli/main.py:267:
src/cli/main.py:268:    Use --mode enterprise for the enterprise recruitment path with inline messaging.
src/cli/main.py:269:
src/cli/main.py:270:    Use --batch-pages to interleave search and messaging every N pages.
src/cli/main.py:271:    Example: -p 10 --batch-pages 2 searches pages 1-2, sends messages,
src/cli/main.py:272:    then pages 3-4, sends messages, etc.
src/cli/main.py:273:
src/cli/main.py:274:    Use --resume to continue from the last interrupted pipeline run.
src/cli/main.py:275:
src/cli/main.py:276:    Examples:\n
src/cli/main.py:277:        maimai pipeline -k "前端工程师" -t greeting -v "recruiter_name=张三" -p 2\n
src/cli/main.py:278:        maimai pipeline -k "前端" -k "后端" -t greeting -v "recruiter_name=张三" --dry-run\n
src/cli/main.py:279:        maimai pipeline -k "前端" -t greeting -p 10 --batch-pages 2\n
src/cli/main.py:280:        maimai pipeline -k "前端" -t greeting -p 1 -i\n
src/cli/main.py:281:        maimai pipeline -k "研发" -t greeting -m enterprise -p 3\n
src/cli/main.py:282:        maimai pipeline --resume
src/cli/main.py:283:    """
src/cli/main.py:284:    from src.core.browser import get_browser_manager
src/cli/main.py:285:    from src.utils.checkpoint import CheckpointManager

src/cli/main.py:287:
src/cli/main.py:288:    # Handle resume mode
src/cli/main.py:289:    if resume:
src/cli/main.py:290:        ckpt = CheckpointManager.load_latest()
src/cli/main.py:291:        if ckpt is None:
src/cli/main.py:292:            console.print("[red]No checkpoint found to resume from.[/red]")
src/cli/main.py:293:            return
src/cli/main.py:294:
src/cli/main.py:295:        from rich.panel import Panel
src/cli/main.py:296:        console.print(Panel(ckpt.summary, title="Resuming Pipeline", border_style="cyan"))
src/cli/main.py:297:
src/cli/main.py:298:        p = ckpt.params
src/cli/main.py:299:        keywords = tuple(p.get('keywords', []))
src/cli/main.py:300:        template = p.get('template', template)
src/cli/main.py:301:        variables = p.get('variables', {})
src/cli/main.py:302:        company = tuple(p.get('company', []))
src/cli/main.py:303:        location = p.get('location', location)
src/cli/main.py:304:        max_pages = p.get('max_pages', max_pages)
src/cli/main.py:305:        batch_pages = p.get('batch_pages', batch_pages)
src/cli/main.py:306:        skip_messaged = p.get('skip_messaged', skip_messaged)
src/cli/main.py:307:        interactive = p.get('interactive', interactive)
src/cli/main.py:308:        mode = p.get('mode', mode)
src/cli/main.py:309:        dry_run = p.get('dry_run', dry_run)
src/cli/main.py:310:    else:
src/cli/main.py:311:        ckpt = None
src/cli/main.py:312:        variables = _parse_variables(var)
src/cli/main.py:313:
src/cli/main.py:314:    if not keywords or not template:
src/cli/main.py:315:        console.print("[red]--keywords (-k) and --template (-t) are required (or use --resume).[/red]")
src/cli/main.py:316:        return
src/cli/main.py:317:
src/cli/main.py:318:    # Resolve SearchMode enum
src/cli/main.py:319:    search_mode = SearchMode(mode)
src/cli/main.py:320:
src/cli/main.py:321:    if search_mode == SearchMode.ENTERPRISE and batch_pages > 0:
src/cli/main.py:322:        console.print("[yellow]Note: --batch-pages with enterprise mode uses infinite scroll; "
src/cli/main.py:323:                      "each batch opens a fresh enterprise search. Deduplication prevents re-messaging.[/yellow]")
src/cli/main.py:324:
src/cli/main.py:325:    _apply_cdp_endpoint(ctx)
src/cli/main.py:326:
src/cli/main.py:327:    async def _pipeline():
src/cli/main.py:328:        from src.modules.auth import ensure_logged_in
src/cli/main.py:329:
src/cli/main.py:330:        reset_delay_session()
src/cli/main.py:331:        browser = get_browser_manager()
src/cli/main.py:332:        try:
src/cli/main.py:333:            await ensure_logged_in(browser)
src/cli/main.py:334:
src/cli/main.py:335:            if batch_pages > 0:
src/cli/main.py:336:                await run_pipeline_batched(
src/cli/main.py:337:                    browser, keywords, company, location,
src/cli/main.py:338:                    max_pages, batch_pages, template, variables,
src/cli/main.py:339:                    dry_run, skip_messaged, interactive, ckpt,
src/cli/main.py:340:                    mode=search_mode,
src/cli/main.py:341:                )
src/cli/main.py:342:            else:
src/cli/main.py:343:                await run_pipeline_default(
src/cli/main.py:344:                    browser, keywords, company, location,
src/cli/main.py:345:                    max_pages, template, variables,
src/cli/main.py:346:                    dry_run, skip_messaged, interactive,
src/cli/main.py:347:                    mode=search_mode,
src/cli/main.py:348:                )

src/cli/main.py:360:    """

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:48:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:49:        Throttle factor ranges from 1.0 (normal) to 0.3 (heavily throttled).
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:50:        - 1 captcha in 30min: reduce to 0.7x (30% fewer operations allowed)
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:51:        - 2 captchas: reduce to 0.5x
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:52:        - 3+ captchas: reduce to 0.3x
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:53:        """

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:55:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:56:        if captcha_count >= 3:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:57:            self._throttle_factor = 0.3
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:58:        elif captcha_count >= 2:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:59:            self._throttle_factor = 0.5
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:60:        elif captcha_count >= 1:

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:62:        else:

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:153:    def check_rate_limit(self, action_type: str) -> None:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:154:        """
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:155:        Check if action is allowed under rate limits.
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:156:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:157:        Args:

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:162:        """

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:164:        if not self._pruned:

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:166:            self._pruned = True
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:167:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:168:        self._refresh_throttle()

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:170:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:171:        now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:172:        one_hour_ago = now - timedelta(hours=1)
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:173:        one_day_ago = now - timedelta(days=1)
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:174:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:175:        # Check hourly limit
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:176:        hourly_count = self._count_actions(action_type, one_hour_ago)
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:177:        if hourly_count >= per_hour:

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:179:            with self.db_manager.session_scope() as session:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:180:                oldest_in_window = session.query(ActionLog.timestamp).filter(
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:181:                    ActionLog.action_type == action_type,
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:182:                    ActionLog.timestamp >= one_hour_ago
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:183:                ).order_by(ActionLog.timestamp.asc()).first()
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:184:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:185:                if oldest_in_window:

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:187:                    wait_seconds = max(1, int((wait_until - now).total_seconds()))
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:188:                else:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:189:                    wait_seconds = 3600
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:190:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:191:            raise RateLimitExceededError(

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:193:                wait_time=wait_seconds,
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:194:                message=f"Hourly rate limit exceeded for {action_type}. "

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:197:

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:252:    def prune_old_entries(self, retention_hours: int = 48) -> int:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:253:        """Remove ActionLog entries older than the retention window.
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:254:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:255:        This prevents stale counts from accumulating across sessions and
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:256:        keeps the ActionLog table from growing indefinitely.
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:257:

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:266:            with self.db_manager.session_scope() as session:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:267:                count = session.query(ActionLog).filter(
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:268:                    ActionLog.timestamp < cutoff
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:269:                ).delete()

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:272:        except Exception as e:

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:276:    def get_quota_status(self, action_type: str) -> dict:

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:278:        Get current quota status for an action type.
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:279:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:280:        Args:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:281:            action_type: Type of action

src/utils/rate_limiter.py:283:        Returns:
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:284:            Dictionary with quota information
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:285:        """
src/utils/rate_limiter.py:286:        per_hour, per_day, _ = self._get_limits(action_type)

src/utils/delays.py:31:def _lognormal_delay(min_val: float, max_val: float) -> float:
src/utils/delays.py:32:    """Generate a log-normal distributed delay between min and max.
src/utils/delays.py:33:
src/utils/delays.py:34:    Log-normal produces a right-skewed distribution: most delays are
src/utils/delays.py:35:    near the low end, with occasional longer pauses — matching human behavior.
src/utils/delays.py:36:    """
src/utils/delays.py:37:    # Map min/max to log-normal mu/sigma
src/utils/delays.py:38:    mid = (min_val + max_val) / 2
src/utils/delays.py:39:    mu = math.log(mid)
src/utils/delays.py:40:    sigma = 0.4  # Controls spread; 0.4 gives moderate variance
src/utils/delays.py:41:    delay = random.lognormvariate(mu, sigma)
src/utils/delays.py:42:    return max(min_val, min(delay, max_val * 1.5))
src/utils/delays.py:43:
src/utils/delays.py:44:
src/utils/delays.py:45:def _fatigue_multiplier() -> float:
src/utils/delays.py:46:    """Calculate fatigue multiplier based on session duration.
src/utils/delays.py:47:
src/utils/delays.py:48:    Humans slow down over time. After 30 minutes, delays increase by ~20%.
src/utils/delays.py:49:    After 1 hour, by ~40%. Caps at 1.6x.
src/utils/delays.py:50:    """
src/utils/delays.py:51:    elapsed_minutes = (time.monotonic() - _session_start) / 60.0
src/utils/delays.py:52:    if elapsed_minutes < 10:
src/utils/delays.py:53:        return 1.0
src/utils/delays.py:54:    # Gradual ramp: 1.0 at 10min → ~1.6 at 90min
src/utils/delays.py:55:    factor = 1.0 + 0.006 * min(elapsed_minutes - 10, 100)
src/utils/delays.py:56:    return min(factor, 1.6)

src/utils/delays.py:60:    """Occasionally return a long "distraction" pause.
src/utils/delays.py:61:
src/utils/delays.py:62:    About 3% chance of a 5-30 second pause (simulating checking phone,
src/utils/delays.py:63:    reading something, etc.). Returns 0 most of the time.
src/utils/delays.py:64:    """
src/utils/delays.py:65:    global _action_count
src/utils/delays.py:66:    _action_count += 1
src/utils/delays.py:67:
src/utils/delays.py:68:    # Don't trigger on first few actions
src/utils/delays.py:69:    if _action_count < 5:
src/utils/delays.py:70:        return 0.0
src/utils/delays.py:71:
src/utils/delays.py:72:    if random.random() < 0.03:
src/utils/delays.py:73:        pause = random.uniform(5.0, 30.0)
src/utils/delays.py:74:        logger.debug(f"Simulating distraction pause: {pause:.1f}s")
src/utils/delays.py:75:        return pause
src/utils/delays.py:76:    return 0.0

src/utils/delays.py:79:def _time_of_day_multiplier() -> float:

src/utils/delays.py:81:
src/utils/delays.py:82:    Late night (23:00-07:00): slower (1.3x) — fewer people browse late.
src/utils/delays.py:83:    Peak hours (10:00-12:00, 14:00-17:00): normal (1.0x).
src/utils/delays.py:84:    Other times: slightly slower (1.1x).

src/utils/delays.py:87:

src/utils/delays.py:90:    elif (10 <= hour <= 12) or (14 <= hour <= 17):
src/utils/delays.py:91:        return 1.0

src/utils/delays.py:164:    """
src/utils/delays.py:165:    Calculate exponential backoff delay for retries.
src/utils/delays.py:166:
src/utils/delays.py:167:    Args:

src/utils/delays.py:176:    delay = min(base_delay * (2 ** attempt), max_delay)
src/utils/delays.py:177:
src/utils/delays.py:178:    # Add jitter (±25%)

src/utils/scoring.py:59:def score_candidate(
src/utils/scoring.py:60:    name: str,
src/utils/scoring.py:61:    title: str,
src/utils/scoring.py:62:    company: str,
src/utils/scoring.py:63:    search_keywords: Optional[List[str]] = None,
src/utils/scoring.py:64:) -> int:
src/utils/scoring.py:65:    """
src/utils/scoring.py:66:    Score a candidate based on title, company, and keyword relevance.
src/utils/scoring.py:67:
src/utils/scoring.py:68:    Higher score = higher priority for messaging.
src/utils/scoring.py:69:
src/utils/scoring.py:70:    Scoring breakdown:
src/utils/scoring.py:71:    - Title seniority: 0-50 points
src/utils/scoring.py:72:    - Company tier: 0-30 points
src/utils/scoring.py:73:    - Keyword match: 0-20 points
src/utils/scoring.py:74:
src/utils/scoring.py:75:    Args:
src/utils/scoring.py:76:        name: Candidate name
src/utils/scoring.py:77:        title: Job title
src/utils/scoring.py:78:        company: Company name
src/utils/scoring.py:79:        search_keywords: Original search keywords for relevance scoring
src/utils/scoring.py:80:
src/utils/scoring.py:81:    Returns:
src/utils/scoring.py:82:        Integer score (higher = better fit)
src/utils/scoring.py:83:    """
src/utils/scoring.py:84:    score = 0
src/utils/scoring.py:85:
src/utils/scoring.py:86:    # 1. Title seniority scoring
src/utils/scoring.py:87:    title_lower = title.lower() if title else ""
src/utils/scoring.py:88:    best_seniority = 0
src/utils/scoring.py:89:    for keyword, points in SENIORITY_SCORES.items():
src/utils/scoring.py:90:        if keyword.lower() in title_lower or keyword in title:
src/utils/scoring.py:91:            best_seniority = max(best_seniority, points)
src/utils/scoring.py:92:    score += best_seniority
src/utils/scoring.py:93:
src/utils/scoring.py:94:    # 2. Company tier scoring
src/utils/scoring.py:95:    # Require minimum 2 characters on both sides to avoid false positives
src/utils/scoring.py:96:    # from short names like "X", "JD" matching substrings of unrelated companies
src/utils/scoring.py:97:    if company:
src/utils/scoring.py:98:        company_lower = company.lower()
src/utils/scoring.py:99:        company_matched = False
src/utils/scoring.py:100:        for t1 in TIER1_COMPANIES:
src/utils/scoring.py:101:            t1_lower = t1.lower()
src/utils/scoring.py:102:            if len(t1_lower) >= 2 and len(company_lower) >= 2:
src/utils/scoring.py:103:                if t1_lower == company_lower or (len(t1_lower) >= 3 and t1_lower in company_lower) or (len(company_lower) >= 3 and company_lower in t1_lower):
src/utils/scoring.py:104:                    score += 30
src/utils/scoring.py:105:                    company_matched = True
src/utils/scoring.py:106:                    break
src/utils/scoring.py:107:        if not company_matched:
src/utils/scoring.py:108:            for t2 in TIER2_COMPANIES:
src/utils/scoring.py:109:                t2_lower = t2.lower()
src/utils/scoring.py:110:                if len(t2_lower) >= 2 and len(company_lower) >= 2:
src/utils/scoring.py:111:                    if t2_lower == company_lower or (len(t2_lower) >= 3 and t2_lower in company_lower) or (len(company_lower) >= 3 and company_lower in t2_lower):
src/utils/scoring.py:112:                        score += 20
src/utils/scoring.py:113:                        break
src/utils/scoring.py:114:
src/utils/scoring.py:115:    # 3. Keyword relevance (if search keywords provided), capped at 20 points
src/utils/scoring.py:116:    if search_keywords and title:
src/utils/scoring.py:117:        keyword_score = 0
src/utils/scoring.py:118:        for kw in search_keywords:
src/utils/scoring.py:119:            kw_lower = kw.lower()
src/utils/scoring.py:120:            if kw_lower in title_lower:
src/utils/scoring.py:121:                keyword_score += 10

src/modules/auth.py:85:async def check_login_status(page: Page) -> bool:
src/modules/auth.py:86:    """
src/modules/auth.py:87:    Check if user is currently logged in by navigating to a protected page
src/modules/auth.py:88:    and observing whether Maimai redirects to the login page.
src/modules/auth.py:89:
src/modules/auth.py:90:    API probes can give false positives (server returns 200 but session is
src/modules/auth.py:91:    actually stale). The redirect-based approach is reliable because Maimai's
src/modules/auth.py:92:    server-side auth check only fires on real page navigations, and it will
src/modules/auth.py:93:    redirect to the login page if the session is invalid.
src/modules/auth.py:94:
src/modules/auth.py:95:    Args:
src/modules/auth.py:96:        page: Playwright page instance
src/modules/auth.py:97:
src/modules/auth.py:98:    Returns:
src/modules/auth.py:99:        True if logged in (no redirect to login page)
src/modules/auth.py:100:    """
src/modules/auth.py:101:    try:
src/modules/auth.py:102:        # Navigate to a protected page that requires authentication.
src/modules/auth.py:103:        # The search center page reliably triggers server-side auth checks.
src/modules/auth.py:104:        protected_url = "https://maimai.cn/web/search_center"
src/modules/auth.py:105:        await page.goto(protected_url, wait_until='domcontentloaded')
src/modules/auth.py:106:
src/modules/auth.py:107:        # Wait for any auth redirect to settle. Instead of a blind 3s wait,
src/modules/auth.py:108:        # watch for URL changes (login redirect) with a shorter timeout.
src/modules/auth.py:109:        try:
src/modules/auth.py:110:            await page.wait_for_url(
src/modules/auth.py:111:                lambda url: 'login' in url.lower(),
src/modules/auth.py:112:                timeout=2000,
src/modules/auth.py:113:            )
src/modules/auth.py:114:            # If we get here, a redirect to login page happened — not logged in
src/modules/auth.py:115:            logger.info(f"Login status check: logged_in=False, detail=redirected_to_login (url={page.url})")
src/modules/auth.py:116:            return False
src/modules/auth.py:117:        except Exception:
src/modules/auth.py:118:            # Timeout = no redirect happened, which is the happy path
src/modules/auth.py:119:            pass
src/modules/auth.py:120:
src/modules/auth.py:121:        # Check 1: URL-based detection - did we get redirected to login?
src/modules/auth.py:122:        final_url = page.url
src/modules/auth.py:123:        if 'login' in final_url.lower():
src/modules/auth.py:124:            logger.info(f"Login status check: logged_in=False, detail=redirected_to_login (url={final_url})")
src/modules/auth.py:125:            return False
src/modules/auth.py:126:
src/modules/auth.py:127:        # Check 2: Page content detection - look for login form elements
src/modules/auth.py:128:        # even if URL didn't change (some login overlays don't change the URL)
src/modules/auth.py:129:        is_login_page = await page.evaluate("""
src/modules/auth.py:130:            () => {
src/modules/auth.py:131:                const bodyText = document.body ? document.body.innerText : '';
src/modules/auth.py:132:                const loginIndicators = [
src/modules/auth.py:133:                    '欢迎使用脉脉',
src/modules/auth.py:134:                    '登录/注册',
src/modules/auth.py:135:                    '请输入手机号',
src/modules/auth.py:136:                    '获取验证码',
src/modules/auth.py:137:                    '扫码登录',
src/modules/auth.py:138:                    '手机号登录'
src/modules/auth.py:139:                ];
src/modules/auth.py:140:                for (const indicator of loginIndicators) {
src/modules/auth.py:141:                    if (bodyText.includes(indicator)) {
src/modules/auth.py:142:                        return { is_login: true, matched: indicator };
src/modules/auth.py:143:                    }
src/modules/auth.py:144:                }
src/modules/auth.py:145:
src/modules/auth.py:146:                // Also check for login form elements in DOM
src/modules/auth.py:147:                const loginForm = document.querySelector(
src/modules/auth.py:148:                    'input[type="tel"], input[placeholder*="手机"], ' +
src/modules/auth.py:149:                    '[class*="qrcode"], [class*="scan-login"]'
src/modules/auth.py:150:                );
src/modules/auth.py:151:                if (loginForm) {
src/modules/auth.py:152:                    return { is_login: true, matched: 'login_form_element' };
src/modules/auth.py:153:                }
src/modules/auth.py:154:
src/modules/auth.py:155:                return { is_login: false, matched: null };
src/modules/auth.py:156:            }
src/modules/auth.py:157:        """)
src/modules/auth.py:158:
src/modules/auth.py:159:        if is_login_page.get('is_login', False):
src/modules/auth.py:160:            detail = is_login_page.get('matched', 'unknown')
src/modules/auth.py:161:            logger.info(f"Login status check: logged_in=False, detail=login_page_detected ({detail})")
src/modules/auth.py:162:            return False
src/modules/auth.py:163:
src/modules/auth.py:164:        logger.info(f"Login status check: logged_in=True, detail=protected_page_accessible (url={final_url})")
src/modules/auth.py:165:        return True
src/modules/auth.py:166:
src/modules/auth.py:167:    except Exception as e:
src/modules/auth.py:168:        logger.error(f"Error checking login status: {e}")
src/modules/auth.py:169:        return False

src/modules/message.py:44:    Only returns IDs that are known to work with the chat URL (u2= parameter).
src/modules/message.py:45:    Query-param IDs (dstu, u2, egid) are reliable for chat navigation.
src/modules/message.py:46:    Path-based IDs (/contact/detail/xxx) are NOT the same as chat user IDs
src/modules/message.py:47:    and should not be used for direct chat URL construction.
src/modules/message.py:48:    """
